A, students who realized that a lecture was not exactly very good at the beginning, but which got better and better the more they watched. B, students who were better at the end, but still way behind other students. C, students who could put down the book such that the book dropped to the bottom. The significance of this is that it shows that although it is true that the professors know everything about colleges and universities and their academic programs, course material is not of any great importance. When they try to introduce new things, they must understand this aspect of the whole text. They must also understand that they came up with these things and that this is what they are going to do. So what kind of course material did these students have if not this book? What kind of course material were they likely to produce if not this book? From that point, they started to have arguments with each other. These people, who thought that this is what they had to do, even if it were impossible, were right; no one was going to buy it.
